\DoxyCodeLine{00688\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ These\ allow\ scalars\ in\ an\ already\ created\ buffer\ to\ be\ updated\ in-\/place.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00689\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Since\ by\ default\ scalars\ are\ stored\ in\ the\ smallest\ possible\ space,}}
